Overview ¶

Package compute aliases all exported identifiers in package "cloud.google.com/go/compute/apiv1/computepb".

Deprecated: Please use types in: cloud.google.com/go/compute/apiv1/computepb. Please read https://github.com/googleapis/google-cloud-go/blob/main/migration.md for more details.
